  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2587340638" />
    <a title="Darlene" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/813598-darlene"><img alt="Darlene" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1201334740p2/813598.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2587340638?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Darlene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Darlene" href="/user/show/813598-darlene">Darlene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=apocalyptic">apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=audible">audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=epidemic">epidemic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=pandemic">pandemic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=horror">horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=zombies">zombies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=humor">humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=survival">survival</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/813598-darlene?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2587340638" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17203640004717474924">While I'm waiting for my characters to come out of hiding, yes, they are literally behind boulders during a volcano as Exploding Ebolic Zombies surround while being shot at by corrupt police... I thought I'd get some of my past due reviews written.<br/><br/>When I was telling my son about my upcoming (and now current) NaNoWriMo zombie novel, he dug out this book. It is an actual handbook that uses some well thought out ways to survive Zombie attacks. It is done tongue in cheek yet if you think about it, t</span>
  <span id="freeText17203640004717474924" style="display:none">While I'm waiting for my characters to come out of hiding, yes, they are literally behind boulders during a volcano as Exploding Ebolic Zombies surround while being shot at by corrupt police... I thought I'd get some of my past due reviews written.<br /><br />When I was telling my son about my upcoming (and now current) NaNoWriMo zombie novel, he dug out this book. It is an actual handbook that uses some well thought out ways to survive Zombie attacks. It is done tongue in cheek yet if you think about it, these ideas could save you during any kind of catastrophe. It is well-written. And the font easy enough for me to read during the day. But since most of my reading happens at night, before bed (yeah, zombies before sleep didn't help much), I added the audible version so I could lean back and really think about what the author was telling us. Marc Cashman narrated this quite well. Though it is written in handbook form the narration was authentic sounding and keeps the reader/listener engaged.<br /><br />I highly recommend this book for those who can take the humor with the survival facts. It will help my future writing as I rethink: how safe are my characters behind those boulders? And where is an exploding zombie when you need one to attack those cops?<br /><br />Oh, just enjoy the book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17203640004717474924" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZMv+ygFoStfkIwZh8tZbss+vJO8snYnpNG8wyH/QiSl6w2pFecyOmNB0PlON5Y9tROkawD5h41bDf4l5td1EyA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EzH+anoEQyRpHlU0q5nof70EtFjJeKAhgPkgbJgDJ/8NOWrlAqCHa11JbQbUqjygNkKKd9uEyp536ZndUg7qHg==')})
  }
//]]>
